Low Silver Prices Unrelated to Shanghai's Silver Reserves 82

The Financial Times Publishes an Article

Reuters 8th, London: The Financial Times today published an article by a Shanghai merchant stating that it is fundamentally wrong to think that China has too much silver. China actually has too little silver. Shanghai does not have sufficient silver to meet the legal requirements for a small number of banknotes. Shanghai now has a large amount of silver because the interior is unstable, so it has gathered here for safety. Once the region is stable and silver needs to circulate, Shanghai's silver reserves will quickly decrease to the point where it is necessary to purchase it from abroad.

Important News

Central Government and National Government Memorial Week 83

Fang Juehui Reports on the Situation in Guizhou Province

Yu Youren Speaks on the Spirit of the Provisional Constitution

The Central Party Headquarters held a memorial week at 9:00 AM on May 8th. Central Committee members Ding Weifen, Fang Juehui, Enhebatou, and all the staff of the Party Headquarters, a total of more than 400 people, attended. Ding Weifen presided over the ceremony. Fang Juehui reported on the inspection of Sichuan and Guizhou provinces, briefly stating: "I have already reported on the inspection of Sichuan Province last time. What I am reporting on today is the general situation in Guizhou Province." The Guizhou Province Party Affairs can be divided into two points: the evolution of party affairs and the current status of party affairs. First, regarding its evolution, there was the organization of the Autonomous Society at the end of the Qing Dynasty, which was the Guizhou branch of the League. The Wuchang Uprising in 1911 was a response by Guizhou, which was due to the activities of that society. Later, due to Tang Jiyao's destruction and Liu Wangzhou's massacre, the party comrades were inevitably displaced. After the reorganization of the party in the 13th year of the Republic, the Premier sent Comrade An Shunqing to Guizhou to prepare for party affairs. In the 15th year of the Republic, the Central Committee sent Zhang Daofan and Li Yizhi back to Guizhou to organize, but Li was eventually killed in Luosi Mountain. In the 17th year of the Republic, the Central Committee sent Ping Gang to Guizhou again as the provincial steering committee to handle registration, but it was dissolved in less than a year. In the 18th year of the Republic, the Central Committee specially sent Li Zhonggong and He Jiwu back to Guizhou to preside over party affairs and determined regular expenses, which led to significant progress. Last year, it underwent another reorganization, which is the current Steering Committee. Then, regarding its current status, the provincial party headquarters has reorganized in accordance with the Central Committee's resolution in February of this year, implementing the system of reducing departments to sections and chiefs of staff. Among the county party headquarters, only Guiyang County has been formally established, organized by the provincial party headquarters to send staff to organize the Guidance Committee Office. There are seven counties. The rest are divided into fifteen party affairs districts throughout the province. Each district includes three to seven counties and establishes a Party Affairs District Commissioner's Office to guide party affairs. This can also be considered a special situation in Guizhou. In terms of party members, only 406 people hold party certificates. Excluding two people who have left the party and 32 people who have left the province, there are only 382 party members in the province. From this, we can imagine the backwardness of Guizhou's culture and the difficulty of developing party affairs. As for party affairs expenses, the provincial party headquarters has 6,000 yuan per month, the Guiyang County party headquarters has 400 yuan per month, the Party Affairs Steering Committee Office has 220 yuan per month, and the Party Affairs District Commissioner's Office has about 300 yuan per month. Mass organizations began to be organized in September of the Yun year [year unclear]. There are 72 officially established organizations of various types. The rest are all being organized due to their simplicity and low standards. From all aspects of party affairs, we can see the backwardness of the border. However, the people of Guizhou are sincere and steadfast once they believe in a doctrine, and they will never change throughout their lives. In addition, there is no reactionary force within the territory, so although there are few party members, the future of party affairs is still promising." Then Fang spoke about the governance of Guizhou Province. The Guizhou Provincial Government is organized in accordance with the regulations of the Central Committee, with the exception of the addition of a military rice office and an advisory office to the secretariat. The advisory office is a special organization to accommodate political talents from the entire province. Its power is higher than the five departments. The salaries of the officials are extremely low. The provincial government chairman only receives 180 yuan per month, and other appointed officials receive between 70 and 18 yuan. Sometimes they are paid only 60% of their salary. Their clean and diligent style is unmatched by other provinces. Then, regarding finance, Guizhou Province's annual income is about 8 million yuan, and annual expenditure requires more than 15 million yuan, a difference of 7 million yuan, so they must vigorously reduce government spending. Then, regarding military affairs, the 25th Army of Mao Guangxiang's department in Guizhou Province originally had more than 60,000 people. After several reorganizations, there are now only three independent brigades, totaling more than 40,000 people. Then, regarding construction, the highways from Guiyang to the four borders have been completed for more than 1,400 li, and there are more than 30 cars. Then, regarding education, elementary schools are the most developed in Guizhou Province, and the number of female students often exceeds the number of male students. This is another special situation for the development of female education in Guizhou Province. The people of Guizhou worship Buddhism and Taoism for religion, but there is very little belief in Christianity. Then, regarding the Miao people, there are 82 types of Miao people in Guizhou Province. Some are named after directions, such as the East Miao and the West Miao. Some are named after clothing colors, such as the Green Miao, White Miao, and Flower Miao. Some are named after their place of residence, such as the Gulong and Longdong. Currently, the number of Miao people in the province is about 800,000, accounting for one-tenth of the Han population. Finally, regarding the feelings after the inspection: (1) The power of the people: Sichuan has done a very good job in handling civil defense forces, which are extremely strong and powerful. There are no bandits to be found anywhere. Guizhou's autonomy has also been quite successful, all due to the power of the people. (2) Road administration: There are many highways in Sichuan, and the highways in Guizhou also reach the four borders. Both use the conscription system and send troops to supervise repairs. One can speed up road construction, and the other can solve the livelihood of the elderly and weak soldiers. Both can be used as models. (3) The suffering of the people: Sichuan's land tax has been collected until the 30th year of the Republic. Taxes are collected according to the region, and the people feel extremely painful. Guizhou is the poorest region in China. Military pay has been assisted by Sichuan with 800,000 yuan, Hunan with 300,000 yuan, and Yunnan with 200,000 yuan. Since the 8th year of the Republic, it has stopped, so the people cannot bear the burden. (4) Characteristics of the military: The Sichuan army immediately declares war when there are conflicts of interest. However, during the war, the generals on both sides can negotiate by telephone, so there is often a war in the morning and peace in the evening, treating the war as a family quarrel. The Guizhou army is different. Once there is a conflict, they will not stop until one side is destroyed. This is the characteristic of the armies in Sichuan and Guizhou provinces. After the report was completed, the ceremony was dismissed.

The National Government held a memorial week at 10:00 AM on the same day. Chiang Kai-shek, Shao Yuanchong, Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, Zhang Jinghui, Wang Shuhan, Wang Boling, Wang Boqun, Jiao Yitang, Enhebatou, Chen Bulei, Liu Shangqing, Chiang Tso-pin, Bao Wen, Zhou Fo, Wang You, Chen Qicai, Lin Xiang, Ru Yuli, Ma Fuxiang, Gong Bingfan, Liu Ruiheng, Zhuang Songfu, Chen Shaokuan, Li Shuhua, Wang Jiazhen, Zhang Wohua, Wu Siyu, and more than 300 officials from the National Government, military aides, accountants, and other offices attended. Chiang Kai-shek presided over the ceremony. Yu Youren spoke, briefly stating: "Convening a national conference and abolishing unequal treaties are two things written in the Premier's will that we will never forget. Because only by convening a national conference can all important domestic problems be solved, and only by abolishing unequal treaties can China be independent in the world. Now the National Conference has closed, and the provisional constitution for the period of political tutelage has also been promulgated by the government. The new life of the Chinese nation begins from this. The spirit of the provisional constitution is completely based on the fundamental principles of the Three Principles of the People. There are detailed provisions on how to solve people's livelihood, how to unite the nation, and how to train and exercise civil rights. However, before implementing the provisional constitution, there must be a pre-negotiated issue, namely, domestic stability and order. If domestic unity hinders order and stability, then we cannot talk about implementing the provisional constitution. In yesterday's letter to the national soldiers, Chairman Chiang reiterated the need to maintain unity and prevent civil war, hoping not to create opportunities for the Red bandits. From this factual evidence, comrades who do not understand should know where the Central Committee's intentions lie. Comrades in the Central Committee should even more sincerely support the Central Committee to achieve complete success. We must all know that the success of this campaign against the Red bandits is the success of Sun Yat-senism and the success of the Republic of China. If it fails, it is the failure of Sun Yat-senism and the failure of the Republic of China. Therefore, at a time when the Red disaster is rampant, all the people of the country and all party members should mobilize in unison and embrace the spirit of 'the past is like yesterday's death, and the future is like today's birth,' dispel misunderstandings, and work together to eliminate the communist bandits in order to complete the national revolution and implement the Three Principles of the People." Secondly, regarding the Supervisory Yuan, the Yuan recently proposed an impeachment case against Sun Weishan, the magistrate of Yuhe County, for illegally collecting waste bone donations. The National Government has clearly ordered the Hebei Provincial Government to thoroughly investigate, but the magistrate plans to publish a rebuttal in Tianjin, believing that the Supervisory Yuan should not impeach the magistrate with two-cent stamps. Little does he know that these two-cent stamps are also paid for by the people. The powers of the Supervisory Yuan are granted by the government. Even without these two-cent stamps, it has the power to impeach. The waste bone donations collected by the magistrate are unheard of in other places. The magistrate's ability to scrape a little oil off waste bones is truly skilled. The magistrate believes that this is a trivial matter, and the Supervisory Yuan does not need to intervene. In fact, this matter is related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. The Supervisory Yuan should propose an impeachment for the sake of exercising its powers. In addition, there is the issue of plowing cattle. Recently, there have been many exports, most of which are food supplies, such as steak. Its impact on agriculture is significant, so in recent years, due to the export of plowing cattle, rich farmers have become middle farmers, middle farmers have become poor farmers, and finally they are displaced. Although the slaughter of cattle was prohibited in the late Qing Dynasty, there were still not enough plowing cattle. If restrictions are not added now, agricultural production will be greatly affected in the future. Some people believe that if there are not enough plowing cattle, they can be replaced by machines. In fact, this method is not applicable to small farmers. I hope that all localities will pay close attention to problems that seem small but are actually of great concern in the future. After the report was completed, the meeting was dismissed.

Deputy Commander Zhang's Illness is Gradually Improving 84

Doctors Say He is Completely Out of Danger

Zhang Qun and Shang Zhen Both Visited the Sick

Beijing Correspondence: Deputy Commander Zhang's condition has gradually improved since he moved to the Union Hospital for quiet recuperation. According to Tianjin Mayor Zhang Xueming and Beijing Mayor Hu Ruoyu, the Deputy Commander's condition as of 12:00 PM the night before (2nd) had dropped to 37.5 degrees Celsius and his pulse was 79, which is very close to normal. He was also able to sleep peacefully at night and was in better spirits than the previous two days. Mayors Zhang and Hu and Zhu Guangmu and others are still taking turns caring for him day and night. He can recover after a quiet rest for ten days. Mrs. Zhang Yu Fengzhi did not go to the hospital to serve him because she also had a cold a few days ago and is currently resting at home.

Yesterday, on the 4th, at 10:00 AM, Chairman Chiang's representative Zhang Qun and Chairman Jin's Shang Zhen went to the Union Hospital to visit Deputy Commander Zhang. After receiving special permission to visit the ward, they expressed their condolences. However, in accordance with the doctor's instructions, they were not allowed to talk, so they immediately withdrew and asked the chief physician about everything before leaving the hospital and returning home. Deputy Commander Zhang's condition, temperature, and pulse were the same as the previous day, and everything went smoothly. According to the doctor, Deputy Commander Zhang is suffering from a mild form of enteric fever, known as [Japanese term] in Japan. The doctor confirmed that he is now completely out of danger. After another two weeks of quiet rest, the fever should subside and he will recover. In general, regardless of who has enteric fever, it must go through three weeks. There is no special treatment method during these three weeks, only quiet rest and not eating, while protecting the heart and waiting for the disease to subside on its own. This type of disease can naturally be cured in more than nine out of ten cases, unless they are particularly weak or do not follow medical advice and eat and move around randomly, causing the intestinal wall to bleed, in which case there is absolutely no danger.

Also, Zhang Qun, after visiting Deputy Commander Zhang, told people that the Deputy Commander's illness had indeed improved yesterday, and his diet was normal. He is now resting quietly and cannot see guests or talk. He is expected to recover within about two weeks. (June 5th)

Year 20 of the Republic of China 85

Regulations for Short-Term Treasury Bonds on Consolidated Taxes

Fixed Amount of 80 Million Yuan. The National Government promulgated on the 6th the Regulations for the Short-Term Treasury Bonds on Consolidated Taxes for the 20th year of the Republic of China. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) These treasury bonds are named "Short-Term Treasury Bonds on Consolidated Taxes for the 20th year of the Republic of China." (Article 2) The fixed amount of these treasury bonds is 80 million yuan, to be used to supplement the national treasury. (Article 3) The fixed monthly interest rate for these treasury bonds is 8%. (Article 4) These treasury bonds will be issued at their full face value, but for the benefit of specially favored purchasers, they may be received at 98% of their value. (Article 5) These treasury bonds will be issued on June 1, 1931. (Article 6) These treasury bonds will be divided into seventy-eight installments for repayment of principal and interest. Starting from June 1931, the monthly principal repayment will be 1% in the first year, 1.1% in the second year, 1.2% in the third year, 1.3% in the fourth year, 1.4% in the fifth year, and 1.5% monthly from the first to fifth month of the sixth year, and 2% in the sixth month, until all are repaid by the end of November 1937. Interest will decrease with the principal. (Article 7) The balance of the cigarette tax collected by the Consolidated Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance and taxes on cotton yarn, wheat flour, etc., are designated as the fund for the principal and interest payments of these treasury bonds. The responsible authorities shall be ordered to transfer the monthly allocated amount to the Central Bank for deposit by the Fund Management Committee, which will also serve as the custodian for payment of principal and interest when due. (Article 8) The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications are designated as the paying agents for these treasury bonds. (Article 9) These treasury bonds are designated as unregistered. (Article 10) These treasury bonds are designated in four denominations: 5,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan. (Article 11) These treasury bonds may be freely mortgaged and traded. They may be used as collateral when security deposits must be paid for official duties. (Article 13) If these treasury bonds are counterfeited or their credit is damaged, the judicial authorities shall punish them according to law. (Article 14)

These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Oppression of Overseas Chinese by Soviet Russia 86

Every Possible Means to Prevent Remittances Home

Those Who Flee the Country Privately Are Shot Dead by Border Guards. Harbin Correspondence: There are frequent reports of Soviet Russia mistreating overseas Chinese. Although the Northeast authorities have repeatedly negotiated, the Russian side has ignored them. This spring, the Russian authorities in Vladivostok confiscated the properties of overseas Chinese such as Wang Rinan. Despite repeated protests from Xu Xiongzhang, the Consul General in Vladivostok, the Russian government has refused to return them, claiming they are in arrears with their taxes. However, this is only the most obvious incident. There are countless others who have been mistreated and unable to return home to complain. Recently, a secret report from a certain consulate in Russia to the Northeast authorities detailed the Russian government's maltreatment of overseas Chinese, causing great indignation. The authorities have issued orders to all agencies in the Northeast to pay close attention and to try to dissuade anyone from going to Soviet Russia again. In addition, Mo Dehui was instructed to negotiate with Russia in the immediate vicinity. The original report from the consulate is recorded below: Since the founding of the Soviet Union, its administration and legislation have been primarily for its own benefit, and its laws and regulations have no permanent nature. What is promulgated today can be repealed tomorrow. It does not consider whether its measures comply with international law or violate morality. Therefore, foreign nationals residing in the Soviet Union, except for those with contractual provisions, are generally at a loss and have no protection for their property or lives. Countless people are groaning in prisons under tyranny. Since the advent of global communication, all foreign nationals who have obtained assets through legitimate labor within the scope of the laws of the host country have been recognized as their property, regardless of the laws of any country or the principles of any legal theory, and they have the right to dispose of them at will. However, the Soviet government, taking the strange view that if Chinese residing in the Soviet Union were allowed to freely accumulate and remit their earnings back home, it would be detrimental to the Soviet treasury, devised a unique and unprecedented example: allowing Chinese to work in the Soviet Union but not allowing them to remit their wages back home. There are no privately established banks in the Soviet Union other than its state-run national bank. The national bank is an agency of the Soviet government, and everything is subject to government orders. When overseas Chinese submit money for remittance, it is invariably rejected. If they attempt to carry it with them when leaving the Soviet Union, it is also prohibited. If wages cannot be remitted back home, the livelihood of overseas Chinese in the Soviet Union is cut off. Therefore, Chinese who used to work as laborers in gold mines and lumberyards have returned home one after another. This happened three years ago. Subsequently, the Soviet Union recruited Russians in places like Linshen, Badai, Bakshe, and Linmuzha to replace them. However, Russians are lazy by nature and not accustomed to hard work. They only work eight hours a day and must be paid extremely high wages, special work clothes, and insurance, etc., which is very costly. The gains are minimal. In less than a year, the gold mines had already suffered heavy losses and had to devise other deceptive tricks to attract Chinese laborers back to work. In 1928, the Soviet Russian government promulgated a special set of regulations: Chinese who go to the gold mines to pan for gold are allowed to remit 75% of their monthly wages back home through a certificate issued by the gold mine's accounting department to the national bank. As a result, overseas Chinese seeking small profits flocked to the area, and the Soviet Union's gold mining industry was revitalized. Once the number of workers in the gold mines was sufficient, the Soviet side reduced the amount of remittances. Initially, it was stipulated that each worker should spend at least 40% or 50% of their wages on food, clothing, and housing in the mine area. Based on this standard, each worker could remit at most 60% or 50% per month. Before long, the Soviet government considered this remittance rate too high and reduced it to only 25% of wages per month. Even after implementing this restriction, it was still considered insufficient. They further exploited the weaknesses of the Chinese by setting up brothels and gambling dens throughout the gold mine areas, enticing the Chinese to indulge so that their wages would be spent as much as possible in the place where they worked. What was gained here was lost here. The baseness of their administration and the insidiousness of their intentions can be said to be the height of their capabilities, and the overseas Chinese who have fallen into this sea of misery have no hope of seeing the light of day again. As for those honest and law-abiding overseas Chinese who are not corrupted by prostitution and gambling and still carefully save their wages, wanting to escape this ominous lair, it is extremely dangerous. Generally, the Soviet gold mines are scattered in sparsely populated areas, located thousands of miles away, obstructed by towering mountains and dangerous rivers with tigers and leopards. Those who do not pass through the official routes rarely return alive. If they carry money through the official routes, they must pass through checkpoints, where they are searched every time they pass through a checkpoint. Any money, gold dust, or other valuables are confiscated. If the amount of confiscated money is large, the person carrying the money is detained and imprisoned. Furthermore, Soviet law requires that a record be made of all confiscated money and property. In addition to recording the facts, if the victim has any objections or statements, they should be included in the record for review. However, when Russians make records, they often do not abide by legal regulations and fabricate Chinese confessions, claiming that the money confiscated from the Chinese was collected from other Chinese in an attempt to smuggle it out of the country. Sometimes, they do not even make a record. The money is confiscated, and the person is released. Whenever overseas Chinese who have suffered this kind of loss report it to the consulate, when negotiations are initiated with the local Soviet officials, for those with records, they cite the fact that the Chinese have already confessed to trying to smuggle it out of the country, so it is naturally confiscated according to regulations and will not be returned. For those without records, the Russian officials simply do not acknowledge that there was any confiscation of money. The Communist Party is barbarous and rogue-like, and it can be said that there is no other like it in the world. Since those who escape are treated in this way, those responsible for protecting overseas Chinese can only stand by empty-handed and shout in vain. It has been found that it is so difficult for Chinese workers in the gold mines to carry money through the official routes that they have to risk taking a detour through the dense forests to try to escape. Those who are fortunate enough not to fall into gullies or encounter leopards and manage to survive to Heihe or other border locations still cannot escape the final danger. Those who obtain official Soviet exit visas and pass through the border checkpoints to return home are subjected to extremely strict searches. Every item and box is opened for inspection. Clothes and bedding are ripped open with scissors, and trunks are split open with iron axes. The person leaving the country is ordered into a special inspection room, where all outer and inner clothing is removed. Men are inspected by male inspectors, and women are inspected by female inspectors. If there are any suspicious signs, they even go as far as doctors examining patients, examining the inside of the lower body. Where is humanity? The insult is extreme. Overseas Chinese with money who do not obtain formal visas and want to escape privately across the frozen Heilongjiang River are constantly patrolled by border guards and cavalry. If a fugitive is spotted, the regulations for martial law are invoked. First, a warning shot is fired to order them to stop. If they do not stop after the warning shot, they can be shot. Only two or three out of ten people who try to escape privately are not captured by the Soviet border guards, and there are frequent reports of people being shot dead by Russian soldiers. Such treatment of overseas Chinese is rarely seen among humans. It has been found that if the Soviet Union does not have Chinese workers, its gold mines and lumberyards cannot be sustained. If they employ Chinese but do not allow them to remit money, even though there are special regulations clearly stipulating that remittances are allowed, in reality, remittances are still not permitted. Once the goal of attracting Chinese workers is achieved, the special regulations are suspended. It is said that the Soviet side is now doing everything possible to prevent Chinese workers in the gold mines from returning home. The Chinese have the obligation to work but not the right to enjoy their wages. This is no different from bandits robbing and kidnapping. The Soviet Union's treatment of our overseas Chinese is so cruel that it is far worse than our treatment of Soviet citizens in northern Manchuria, who are treated with kindness and given clear legal protection. If we do not treat this barbaric government in the same way that they treat our overseas Chinese, I fear they will never realize their error. According to the principle of international equality and reciprocity, it seems appropriate to adopt the same methods to treat them. (4th)

Shanxi Court Burns Opium 87

Opium Spreads in Shanxi, No. 1 in the Nation

Annual Losses of Several Tens of Millions of Yuan. Taiyuan Correspondence: Yesterday was the anniversary of Commissioner Lin Zexu's burning of opium. The Shanxi Higher and Local Courts specially invited representatives from party, government, military, academic, newspaper, and other organizations to the Zhongshan Park at 2:00 PM yesterday to jointly supervise the burning of a large batch of opium and drugs. A total of over 6,700 taels of processed opium and opium dross, over 6,000 taels of raw materials for "golden pills," 126 boxes and over 20 bags of packaged opium were burned, totaling over 10,000 taels of drugs and 67 baskets of smoking paraphernalia and other sundries. According to court statistics, the items burned this time were seized in the past two years. The total amount of processed opium seized in the past two years exceeds the total amount seized in the ten years from 1919 to 1928 by over 1,000 taels, proving that the amount of opium in Shanxi has increased sharply in recent years. It is estimated that the value of the items burned this time is over 3 million yuan. However, the amount of drugs seized by the authorities is only one or two percent of the total. Moreover, the opium seized over the years has all been sent to the village administration for the distribution of peace opium cessation medicine, which is also a huge sum. Based on this, it can be imagined how much money is being lost from Shanxi every year. It has been found that most of the drugs seized in recent years are raw materials for "golden pills" and processed opium, indicating that Shanxi has definitely shifted from trafficking to manufacturing. The danger of the situation is truly alarming. Therefore, the public was extremely enthusiastic about attending the burning yesterday. First, the court transported the various drugs in batches to the park in many large carts and displayed them for everyone to view. Then, Shao Xiuwen, the president of the Higher Court, presided over the memorial meeting. Over 200 representatives attended. After paying respects, Shao and Wu Zhenduo, a representative from the Anti-Drug Association, gave speeches. Shao's succinct words were that if the "golden pills" and opium dross are not eliminated, the people of Shanxi will be wiped out in a few decades. The prevalence of "golden pills" and opium dross is definitely the highest in Shanxi. The burning began around 4:00 PM and the event was adjourned. June 4th.

Mr. Ma Yinchu's Opinion on the Private Bank Law (Continued) 88

This is a general report on the issue of the Private Bank Law. I believe that there is no reason to draft this law, because the private banking industry does not primarily focus on lending on credit. Is it the same as a bank in terms of business? Because banks engage in the business of accepting deposits and lending, and private banks also engage in the business of accepting deposits and lending. Banks engage in the buying and selling of raw gold, and private banks also engage in the buying and selling of raw gold. We cannot think of any differences between them, so it is difficult to regulate them separately. If separate regulations are made, then in the future, for social occupations, there will also have to be a Barber Law for barbers, a Rickshaw Puller Law for rickshaw pullers, and a Tailor Law for tailors, which will be too numerous to handle. Since the businesses done by banks and private banks are of the same nature, we have included them together. If their natures are different, then of course separate regulations can be made. To ask where the current business done by private banks differs from that of banks, the only difference is that private banks cannot issue banknotes, while banks can issue banknotes. However, private banks in the interior also issue paper money, and regarding this aspect, we will gradually eliminate the right of commercial banks to issue banknotes in the future. Therefore, although banks and private banks have different names, they are actually the same. There is no need to draft a separate Private Bank Law. This is my opinion on the Private Bank Law. Since the promulgation of the Banking Law, private banks have believed that Article 1 of the Banking Law includes private banks, considering private banks to be subordinate to banks. This is a great misunderstanding. We believe that if a private bank is reorganized into a general partnership, then the position of a general partnership is above that of a bank organized as a joint-stock company. Why do we say this? A general partnership not only requires the pooling of capital but also requires each person to contribute their labor in order to succeed. It places emphasis on what is called personality, and therefore it can be called a Personality Company. Not just anyone can become a shareholder. It is necessary to see what the shareholder's personality is like. The person must be talented, or morally upright, or have a high reputation. Only when the person's personality is high can the company be valued by society. If the personality of the shareholders is not valued, then the company will also be affected. From this point of view, the personality of the shareholders is greatly related to the company, so it can be called a Personality Company. On the contrary, almost all current banks are organized as joint-stock companies, and joint-stock companies are completely opposite to general partnerships. It does not matter who becomes a shareholder. As long as the prescribed share capital is paid, the moral value of the person can be completely ignored. Even the directors of the company are not directly responsible for the debts. The entity responsible is the joint-stock company itself. Joint-stock companies must solicit share capital from all over the world and cannot investigate each individual's character and personality before admitting them as shareholders. The reason is that a general partnership is established by a small number of people who know each other well, so they can gather people with a high level of credit. As for joint-stock companies, their shares can be bought and sold at any time, so today's shareholder may be a respectable person, but tomorrow he may sell his shares to someone with a questionable personality. All is unknown. Therefore, if one must investigate personality, then the company will only not succeed. The company cannot control the personality of the shareholders. In essence, joint-stock companies have no relationship to personality. They only pool capital, so they can be called Capital Companies. From this, it can be seen that a general partnership is a Personality Company and a joint-stock company is a Capital Company. It can be seen that the position of a general partnership is far above that of a joint-stock company. How can it be said that a private bank is subordinate to a bank? In legal terms, one emphasizes personality and one emphasizes capital. One who emphasizes personality is naturally above one who emphasizes capital. Therefore, the Banking Law does not regard private banks as subordinate to banks. (End)

Hangzhou Express News 89

Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Nanxian telegraphed the 3rd Security Regiment stationed in Changshan and the county magistrates of the Quzhou region to intensify defense in order to prevent the Gan bandits from infiltrating, and separately ordered the county clearance bureaus to ensure the thoroughness of household registration investigations and joint guarantees.

The Army Hospital stationed in Hangzhou under the Ministry of Military Affairs was ordered to issue half a month's salary and a third-class travel pass to all wounded and sick officers and soldiers who have recovered, and return them to their original divisions, brigades, regiments, and battalions. The Military Department also dispatched Zhou Kaiji and Wen Renjia to Hangzhou to call the roll and issue instructions at the Genshan Station, ordering them not to linger in Hangzhou and damage the reputation of the military.

The Department of Civil Affairs has instructed the Pujiang county magistrate, Lü Siyi, to investigate and deal with the complaint from Pujiang citizen Jin Youguang, accusing him of dereliction of duty, harming the people, and disregarding human life, and the complaint from Kaihua citizen He Dequan, accusing the county magistrate Mao Gaokun of allowing police to cross borders to harass and rob people.

The second principal repayment lottery for the Zhejiang Provincial Disaster Relief Public Bonds will be held by the Department of Finance on the 15th of this month at the Hangzhou City Chamber of Commerce.

A large-scale rent resistance riot by farmers in Shangyu has erupted. County Magistrate Zhang Jingxi has arrested eight ringleaders, including Lü Bingzhang, and handed them over to the provincial court for trial. The county's fellow-townsmen association in Beijing has telegraphed the provincial government, presenting the details of the case and requesting a prompt hearing for those arrested to avoid harming others. They have also sent a letter to the court for reference.

Qingyuan County Magistrate Huang Shijie proposed at the current Construction Administration Conference that mushroom cultivation is a major source of income for farmers in the old Quzhou area (Longquan, Jinyun, Qingyuan), amounting to approximately one million yuan per year. However, in recent years, the mushroom forests in Qingyuan County have been depleted, and the livelihoods of mushroom farmers are becoming increasingly precarious. He urged the implementation of mushroom forest cultivation. The Department of Construction has ordered the governments of the ten counties in the old Quzhou area to investigate the local situation and promptly submit plans for review and approval. (8th)

Tobacco Industry and Brick & Tile Industry Establish Trade Associations. Eighteen industries have already established trade associations in the city and are forming a chamber of commerce preparatory committee to register members for the establishment of a new chamber of commerce. Today (the 8th), the Tobacco Industry and the Brick & Tile Industry also established trade associations. The county party headquarters sent Wu Guofang and the county government sent Qian Tiansheng to the establishment meeting at the chamber of commerce to supervise the election. Fan Changding presided over the election for the Brick & Tile Industry, and the results were that Fan Changding, Wang Zuoyi, Zhang Shouliang, and others were elected as executive committee members.

In order to obtain accurate information, it is necessary to conduct a new review. Orders have been issued to the district chiefs to instruct the township and town police to investigate and report the names of the townships, towns, and villages within the county's borders within a limited time.

Suzhou 91

Chambers of Commerce in Various Industries Discuss Business Tax. The issue of business tax in Wu County has not been resolved due to the fact that the tax rate and amount have not been determined, so it is still in stalemate. Now that the Business Tax Law has been promulgated, the county chamber of commerce specially convened a meeting of representatives from various industries on the 8th. Sixty-seven representatives from forty industries attended. Chairman Shi Junqing reported that the chamber of commerce had previously entrusted Cheng Ganqing to go to the provincial finance department to contact Section Chief Chen, but to no avail. The Business Tax Bureau has sent a declaration form requesting assistance, and it has been distributed to various businesses with the hope that they will accurately fill it out and submit it to the chamber within the deadline. It was resolved that (1) the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce should be consulted on the progress of the business tax and whether the reported business tax rate has been submitted to the ministry for review. (2) The county chambers of commerce should be contacted to inquire whether they have expressed any opinions on the provincial and municipal tax rates and the starting date for collection. Paying the Busy Season Grain Tax Must Not Be Done Privately. Yuan Xiaogu, the Director of the Finance Bureau, stated that because the deadline for the busy season grain tax in the old Changyuan and Wu counties had passed, the tax receipts for each household should follow the old procedure of being collected and issued by the financial police, who would hold a list of each precinct and press each household to pay the tax within a fixed time limit. The director is now cutting off the process of issuing tax receipts and demanding payment and has presented the order to the county magistrate and district chiefs to inform the township and town chiefs and deputy propaganda officers to inform the grain households. If the tax collectors holding the unpaid tax receipts come to collect the busy season grain tax, they should promptly pay it and must obtain the tax receipts from the tax collector. If the payment is made to the tax collector but the tax receipts are not obtained, they must not entrust others to pay on their behalf privately. If the tax collector embezzles the money, the rice-growing household shall be responsible. County Magistrate Huang, upon receiving the report, ordered the district chiefs to comply with the order yesterday.

The Entire Committee for Soliciting Public Bonds Resigns. County Magistrate Huang of Wu County, in order to comply with the order to solicit 200,000 yuan in construction public bonds, immediately hired Zhang Yi and 14 others to serve as solicitation committee members and organized a committee to carry out the solicitation. However, the committee members believed that this construction public bond was not for use in Wu County but for construction in various counties in Jiangbei, and that Wu County had already shouldered construction surcharges and various public bonds last year, and the burden on the public was already extreme. They were unable to bear the construction public bond again. On the 8th, they separately presented a letter to the county government, the finance department, and the provincial government, expressing their collective resignation.

Wuxi 92

Counterfeit Banknotes of a Certain Bank Mixed in the Market. Although this year's silkworm cocoon market is not even two-tenths of what it was last year, the market is still slightly lively. Unexpectedly, large numbers of counterfeit five-yuan banknotes of a certain bank have been mixed in the city in recent days. Criminals are using them to purchase small items from various merchants, and the number of victims is unknown. According to investigations by reporters, some of the criminals using counterfeit banknotes are dressed luxuriously and wear gemstone rings, while the rest are mostly young children. The Sun Siquan incense shop and others outside the North Gate Altar Lane have been victimized by purchasers who bought items worth only a few jiao and paid with counterfeit five-yuan banknotes. Countless other shops have also been victimized. The public security authorities have begun investigations and are asking to prevent speculation by silk factories. Hui Jizhi, the standing director of the joint council of the local silk factory industry and labor union, believes that most entrepreneurs in various places are engaging in industry by being cunning and opportunistic, raising a small amount of capital and then renting a factory to start work. They then use this to attract loans and treat their workers as slaves. They pay no attention to the necessary equipment stipulated by factory laws. Fortunately, if they are successful and become rich, they see their methods as a shortcut to wealth and adhere to them without making any improvements. Unfortunately, if they suffer a setback, they simply flee. Those who are cunning and fraudulent become entangled in lawsuits, affecting people's livelihoods, disrupting the industry, disrupting the social economy, and harming workers' welfare. This is the most serious problem. During the previous attendance at the National Assembly, it was proposed that the central government stipulate by law the minimum amount of capital and the minimum necessary equipment for establishing a factory, and that the responsible departments should inspect and verify this to prevent speculation, harm to the industry, and harm to workers' welfare. The proposal was passed. Speculation is most prevalent in silk factories. Now that the silkworm cocoon market is about to open, if this case is not regulated and implemented, not only will speculators continue to mingle in the market, but it will also be difficult to improve the necessary equipment. Therefore, the original proposal was attached yesterday and presented to County Magistrate Pan for review and approval. The proposal requests that the provincial government forward the case to the National Government and the responsible departments to promptly investigate the matter, stipulate the method of implementation, and order the provincial governments to instruct their subordinates to inspect and verify it in order to prevent speculation and maintain the industry.

Qingpu 93

A Murder Case Occurred Due to Adultery. Chen Jingren, a peddler in the Nanxun area of Huangdu Town, Tenth District, owned a Jiangbei boat. Chen's wife was known to be promiscuous and had recently become intimate with her husband's friend, Wang Xiaoru. However, they were unable to do as they pleased due to Chen's presence. On the night before last, around 12:00 AM, Wang lured Chen to the Taji Bridge on the Qingbai District and shot him dead. Wang then fled. The local security corps reported the incident and immediately dispatched corps members to hire civilian boats to join the town's security corps in arresting the criminal, but he had already vanished without a trace.

Bandits in Chaidang Village Mistakenly Injure a Comrade. Around 8:00 PM the night before last, several bandits suddenly arrived in Chaidang Village, Eighth District, firing shots to show their power. They were about to rob the village when the villagers heard the noise and beat gongs to warn the others. They also rushed to report to the district corps headquarters. District Corps Chief Dai immediately led his men to pursue the bandits, who had already fled. Before leaving, they mistakenly injured one of their comrades, who was lying in a pool of blood, on the verge of death. A pistol and bullets were found on his body. The wounded bandit was taken to the Baihejiang Hospital for treatment, but he died the next morning due to his severe injuries. The county government reported the incident, and Investigator Guo Enguang personally led an examination team to investigate. They found that the deceased had indeed been shot to death. The local authorities were ordered to provide a coffin for burial.

Kunshan 94

An Entertainment Venue Almost Caused a Disaster. The local theater has been repeatedly closed due to poor business. Since the local resident Ma Jikang organized the Public Entertainment Venue in the spring, it has catered to the social psychology and business has been very prosperous. However, conflicts between audience members often arise inside the venue. Last night, several audience members from other places disagreed with a local carpenter named A Bing and beat him severely, causing him serious injuries. Fortunately, the staff of the venue tried their best to mediate and the group dispersed. During the beating, the audience members in the entire venue rushed to escape through the doors, causing great chaos and almost causing a disaster. After Qin Jieren, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, learned of the incident, he immediately dispatched Inspector Gu Yingqiu to investigate. According to eyewitnesses, a certain squad leader was involved. He immediately returned to the bureau to report. Therefore, from today onwards, the Public Security Bureau and the county police team will send armed police officers to protect the venue day and night to prevent further incidents.

Fengxian 95

Regarding the request to merge the contiguous areas of Songjiang and Nanhui counties into this county, namely the Taiping Township Songkou and Tuolinjiang areas of Nanhui, the local party and government have repeatedly and strongly advocated for their incorporation, but approval has not yet been granted. The current county government believes that the newly promulgated "Outline for the Reorganization of County Administrative Regions" and its stipulations regarding mergers and divisions are highly suitable for the situation in these two areas. Therefore, it is reiterating the previous proposal and requesting provincial review and approval. Simultaneously, regarding the Nanhui-owned Minhang Duipu Sanli's South Min route, a telegram has also been sent to the Construction Department requesting permission to first incorporate it into Fengxian to expedite its completion.

A Salt Farmer from Shiniu Group Was Secretly Murdered: Li Wenxiang, a salt farmer from the Shiniu Group in this county's salt field area, was invited from his home on the 18th of last month by several people, including a patrolman named Zhang from the Pujiang Patrol Team's boat. They invited him to a small teahouse in Shiqiaotou for entertainment. Unexpectedly, he disappeared without a trace, and despite repeated searches by his family, no whereabouts were found. Then, the tax collection official of the 11th Group suddenly discovered a corpse in an empty room in Heshangtang. He immediately reported it to the county government, which dispatched personnel to the countryside for inspection. The results confirmed that he had been secretly murdered. The family of the deceased believes that Patrolman Zhang has a significant connection to the case, so they came to the county yesterday to report and request an investigation.

Changzhou 96

A Ship Was Robbed in Nanshu, Wujin: A ship from Nanshu, Wujin County, loaded with passengers and goods in the town, was traveling at 2 AM on the 6th. When passing the Jindaqiao in Qishan Township, the Sixth District, it was suddenly attacked by armed bandits. The robbery lasted for about half an hour before the bandits went ashore with their loot. Afterwards, the Shipping Association reported the incident to the county government on the 7th, requesting the apprehension of the thieves.

Changshu 97

Residents of Liuhai Attacked Survey Team: The waterway for flood discharge from the lower reaches of the Sigan River in Shazhou City of this county must pass through the Liuhai Sandbank, which belongs to Nanhui County. Therefore, Chen Qiwei, the Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, went to Nantong before the Sigan River was dredged to have an in-depth discussion with the Nanhui County Magistrate and the Director of the Construction Bureau regarding the river's flood discharge issue. As a result, an agreement was reached with Nantong to take a shortcut into the Yangtze River between the five and six Weirs bordering the Jisheng Case and the Yicheng Case of Liuhai. This was then submitted to the provincial departments for approval. The dredging of the lower reaches of the Sigan River has now reached a satisfactory stage in this county, but the dredging of the flood discharge route is urgently needed. This county dispatched a survey team led by Zhao Wenxuan to the countryside to start the survey. Unexpectedly, when Zhao arrived at the sandbank and was about to begin work, two to three hundred residents of Liuhai surrounded the survey team, creating a threatening situation and prohibiting the survey. When Zhao refused to comply, a conflict arose. The surveying equipment Zhao brought was destroyed, and the surveyor Chen Yusheng was taken away and his whereabouts are unknown. After receiving the report, the Director of the Construction Bureau of this county has already requested compensation from Nantong and has sent a telegram to the provincial departments reporting the incident and requesting instructions.

Nantong 98

County Magistrate Zhang Requests Instructions and Returns to Nantong: Nantong County Magistrate Zhang Dong recently went to the province to seek instructions on various important local issues concerning public security, finance, and vehicle donations. He returned to Nantong on the 7th and made the following statements: (1) The disaster in the rural areas has not been quelled, and the district heads have no protection when handling cases, so they have submitted their resignations collectively. The county government is currently unable to concurrently handle judicial affairs, making it difficult to deal with banditry cases. Chairman Ye has agreed to provide relief during this visit and has approved the proposal for county magistrates of Nantong, Wujin, and other counties to be temporarily exempted from concurrently handling judicial affairs, according to a provincial telegram. (2) Nantong's provincial tax revenue is 90,000 yuan per year, but expenditures reach over 200,000 yuan per year. The Director of the Finance Bureau cannot help but misappropriate special funds, and it has become a common practice for various departments to send telegrams to detain funds upon his transfer. This time, it was approved that the Finance Department should limit the issuance of payment orders in the future. (3) Regarding the strike against donations for automobiles and rickshaws, the Construction Department stated that the drivers must first register and pay off the outstanding donations before the donation reduction can be approved. The provincial government has not yet received any telegrams from the headquarters regarding the matters of wounded soldiers and factories.

Police Officers Throughout the County Strive for Public Safety Acreage Donation: Police officers throughout Nantong County are striving for the Public Safety Acreage Donation, which has already raised 120,000 yuan, but has actually been completely misappropriated by the Fund Management Office. They are currently requesting funds from the office, and if there are no results, they will petition the province.

Zhenjiang 99

Public Security Bureau Bans the Society for the Prohibition of Opium and Alcohol: The Public Security Bureau of the Jiangsu Provincial Capital, having received a letter from the Zhenjiang County Party Department stating that the Zhenjiang Lishentang's society for the prohibition of opium and alcohol is a disguised form of the Li Sect and that the Cishantang worships idols to confuse the foolish. It is ostensibly promoting the prohibition of opium and alcohol but is secretly opening halls to recruit disciples, essentially a variation of the White Lotus and Red Lantern sects. The Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department has long issued orders to the County Civil Affairs Bureau to ban it. Recently, the society has resumed large-scale activities in the Xiaomenghu area, extensively recruiting followers. Such illegal gatherings not only promote superstition and confuse the masses but also have a significant impact on society. Therefore, it should be banned immediately. The Bureau specially ordered the Fifth Sub-Bureau to comply.

A Strange Doctor's Injection Kills a Person: Li Yousheng, a worker on the Jingji Lingdong Railway, was visited yesterday by a doctor claiming to be a local named Liu Qingquan. He carried a leather bag containing instruments and syringes and insisted on treating Li's wife. Only Li's wife was home at the time, and she was not ill, only physically weak. Dr. Liu said that she would become strong after an injection. However, as soon as the injection was given, Li's wife lost consciousness. Neighbors, realizing that a life was at stake, reported the incident to the police post, who arrested the doctor and transferred him to the Seventh Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau, who in turn transferred him to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Gaoyou 100

Township Head Chen's Daughter-in-Law Was Kidnapped but Escaped: The family of Chen Lianggui, the township head of An'nan Township in the Fifth District of this county, was suddenly attacked by many bandits in the latter part of last month. After looting, they kidnapped his daughter-in-law, Ms. Guo, and took her to the bandit den at Wangjia Bridge in Bao'ying. The night before last, Ms. Guo took advantage of the captors' sleepiness and slipped out the back door, escaping back under the cover of darkness. It is now reported that the Chen family, fearing the bandits' return, plans to move to the city temporarily for shelter.

Jingjiang 101

A Ransom Victim Escaped from a Kidnapping Case in Banzha: Many people were kidnapped during a bandit raid in Banzha Town, Huai'an. The police teams of Huai'an and Lianshui counties jointly searched the area within Lianshui County but failed to rescue them. Then, on the 29th of the previous month, Wang Haicen, the leader of the Lianshui Temporary Guerrilla Team, received a report that Zhang Tingyuan's house in Zhangzhuang, at the border between Huai and Lian, was hiding kidnapped victims. He immediately led a team to search and found a cellar in Tingyuan's kitchen. In addition to arresting Tingyuan and a bandit named Liu Fengwu, they also rescued five kidnapped victims from the cellar: He Xiuwen from Banzha, two boys from Zhang Zhankui's family, a boy from Ren Kaifu's family in Huai'an, and two boys from Zhu Liwu's family in Sanliwan, Huai'an. Lin Jing, the County Magistrate of Huai'an, immediately dispatched Zhi Xiaoshun, the captain of the First Police Squad, to Lianshui to escort them back. The families of the kidnapped victims have already received them from the county government over the past two days.

Bandits Murder Merchants: Gan Weifan, from Ganzhuang, north of the Yan River in the Third District of Huaiyin, has been running a small shop in Yuanji. He is now fifty years old. The day before last, several bandits suddenly went to Yuanji, dragged Gan out of his shop, and shot him. The entire town was in turmoil. Only after the bandits left did Gan's wife, Ms. Zhang, carry his body back for burial. The reason for his murder, according to outsiders, was revenge by the bandits.

Yangzhou 102

Public Security Bureau Seizes Large Quantity of Smuggled Salt: The Ninth Sub-Bureau of the Dayi Public Security Bureau in this county received a secret report the day before yesterday stating that Zhao Zi's house in Wangzhuang, several dozen li northeast of the town, was hiding a large quantity of smuggled salt and requested to be dispatched for a search. Upon receiving the report, the Bureau immediately dispatched police officers accompanied by the informant. They indeed discovered more than one hundred packages of smuggled salt. They immediately dispatched police to guard it and took Zhao Zi to the Bureau to await transfer to the county for punishment.

Luhe 103

Provincial Commissioners Investigate the Truth of the Education Tide and All School Teachers Resign Collectively: The teachers' collective resignation has lasted for two weeks, and education throughout the county has been suspended. After County Magistrate Liu's mediation, they agreed to pay one and a half months' salary before the Dragon Boat Festival, and all teachers reluctantly returned to class on June 3. Yesterday, the Education Department sent Qin Fengxiang to Luhe to investigate the commission of three points: (1) The status of the education budget; (2) The cause of this incident; (3) The truth about the mutual beatings between Education Commissioner Qian Zhiyao and Principal Zhang Kaifa. They also convened a discussion meeting with educators at the Second Public Reading Society to discuss solutions.

Hangzhou 104

Bandit Leader Lan Zhengxing Was Killed: Lan Zhengxing, a bandit leader from Jingning in this province, has been burning, killing, and looting the local residents, who hate him to the bone. A month ago, he shot and killed the Mei Yongyan family and others, a total of five lives, and all their property was looted. The province repeatedly issued strict orders to intensify the pursuit. After learning that the bandit was hiding in Rigecun, Yuan Xuchu, the captain of the county government's patrol team, led troops to secretly arrest him late at night. At midnight, they arrived at their destination and dispatched troops to guard the entrances. The captain suddenly attacked and shot the bandit in the abdomen. The bandit was caught off guard and was seriously wounded while trying to escape to the roof. He then fell from the roof due to his injuries and died. The people were overjoyed. The County Magistrate telegraphed the province to report yesterday.

A Child Was Kidnapped But Released Midway: Jin Aniu, the owner of the Jin Dachang Hotel in Youcheqiao, three li from Shangqianbu, had some savings, which aroused the envy of bandits. The night before last, six bandits suddenly came with the intention of kidnapping Aniu's son, but mistakenly entered the neighboring Jin Zhangsheng's house and kidnapped Jin's child. When they reached Tanjia Ferry, the bandits realized their mistake and abandoned the kidnapped victim on the road, leaving with a howl.

The Provincial Clearing and Suppression Bureau Executes a Bandit: Zhang Maoxing, a twenty-year-old from Yongkang, had previously colluded with Chen Baofang and others, who were at large, and robbed Yin Qian and silverware from the home of Gu Baishun in Gaodi, Yuyue, while armed with guns. They also went to Nanmiao to rob gold rings from Lu Rongqing and Zhang Shuijin. Last month, they were arrested by the local police and security team, and a kidnapped victim, Zhang Shaoxin, was rescued. After the Clearing and Suppression Bureau interrogated him and confirmed the facts, they specially requested the Provincial Clearing and Suppression Headquarters to consult with the provincial government for approval. He was executed by firing squad yesterday. Educational News Highlights

Stalemate in Tsinghua Student Unrest 105

Wu Nanxuan Continues to Submit Resignation: Beijing, 8th. A central telegram stated that the Tsinghua student unrest has reached a stalemate. Professors and students are strongly opposed to Wu. Wu has continued to submit his resignation to the Ministry of Education, but he is determined not to abandon his responsibility before it is approved. Wu stated that running a school requires the use of tactics, which is an unprecedented phenomenon in various countries. Yu Ning is a victim of other people's tactics and does not want to use tactics to destroy righteousness. The Ministry of Education also telegraphed Jiang Menglin, hoping that he would take into consideration the government's prestige and quickly quell the school's student unrest, and ordered him to handle it with full authority. Jiang went to the school yesterday to consult with the professors and decided on several measures, which will be reported to the Ministry of Education for instructions before they can be resolved.

Ministry of Education Explains Matters Concerning Student Self-Government Associations 106

The Ministry of Education urgently instructed the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education that the Nantong County Education Bureau reported that the promulgated "Outline of the Student Self-Government Association" and its implementation rules had been followed by all schools under its jurisdiction. However, after examining Article 2 of the implementation rules, the term "competent authority" in the "Outline of the Student Self-Government Association" refers to the county government in counties and the municipal government in cities, which is the same as the example in Article 10, Paragraph 3 of the Education Association Law, which states that the supervisory body of the County Education Association and its District Education Association is the county government. Currently, communications between the Education Association and the Education Bureau still use orders and reports, and the same format is used between the Education Bureau and the Student Self-Government Association. It seems that the precedent of communications between the Education Bureau and the Education Association should be followed, but there is no clear written regulation, so they dare not make a decision without authorization. The Ministry of Education instructed: "Received the report. The format of communications between the Education Bureau and the Student Self-Government Association may follow the example of communications between the Education Bureau and the Education Association, using orders and reports. Inform and instruct accordingly."

The Ministry of Education also received a report from the Shandong Provincial Department of Education, which reported that the Taian County Magistrate telegraphed to request instructions on whether the design of the Student Self-Government Association's emblem should be issued according to the designs of other labor unions. The Ministry of Education instructed: "Received the report. The regulations for the production of emblems for social organizations have already been promulgated by this Ministry's Order No. 750. According to the provisions of the revised plan for people's organizations, the Student Self-Government Association is a social organization, so the design of the emblem should comply with these regulations for the production of emblems for social organizations. Inform and instruct accordingly."

Ministry of Education's Approval of the Request to Restore Medical and Pharmaceutical Vocational Schools 107

The Ministry of Education instructed the request from the Medical and Pharmaceutical Association of the Republic of China to establish a medical and pharmaceutical education system and restore medical and pharmaceutical vocational schools: "Received the report. In August of the 18th year, the regulations for vocational schools promulgated by this Ministry originally included the provision for pharmaceutical vocational schools. The recent revision of these regulations has added a medical vocational school. The report was submitted to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government for filing and notification to all departments and bureaus and all vocational schools. In addition to the medical colleges or independent medical departments established by the regulations for universities, this Ministry also allows the establishment of medical and pharmaceutical vocational schools. The old medical and pharmaceutical vocational schools can be reorganized and continued based on their original foundation in accordance with the Vocational School Organization Law and the revised vocational school regulations. Inform accordingly."

Superintendent of Schools in Jiangsu Province Inspects Qingpu Education Bureau 108

Since Yuan Weiwen became the Director of the Qingpu Education Bureau, he has spared no effort in promoting all undertakings. When Provincial Superintendent Xu Weichu arrived in Qingpu the other day to inspect, he was very satisfied with the work of the bureau. It is also reported that the bureau will hold the county's middle and elementary school graduation examinations on the 14th of this month.

Jiading Normal School Will Hold Its 30th Anniversary Celebration 109

Jiading Private Normal School was founded during the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. At that time, the people's spirit had not yet been opened, but the school was unique in its creation. It has been drifting through wind and rain for thirty years. The teaching is effective and the school spirit is strict, so the talents cultivated are abundant in society. The school's 30th anniversary celebration will be held in mid-July for two days with grand commemorative meetings, such as film performances, new dramas, broadcasting, achievement exhibitions, full gatherings and large lantern parties. At that time, regardless of the old and young alumni, they will all hold two lanterns each and rejoice.

Li Gongying Takes the Lead in this Year's Bank Club Billiards Tournament 118

Won the Du Xigui Silver Cup with a score of 700 to 349 in last night's finals, defeating Shen Lince. The Bank Club's billiards (pocket) tournament has a history of more than three years. The participants are mostly giants in the banking industry and leaders in commerce and industry, who engage in this beneficial physical exercise in their spare time. Among them, some have high skills and some have deep experience. Each competition adopts a handicap system, so equal opportunities increase interest. In this year's handicap billiards tournament, there were 28 contestants. After several rounds, only Li Gongying and Shen Lince remained. The finals were held at 6:15 PM yesterday. As a result, Li Gongying defeated Shen Lince with a score of 700 to 349. Mr. Du Xigui's large silver cup was won by Mr. Li, and he was awarded the championship souvenir. The runner-up, Shen Lince, also received a silver cup from the department. The details of each item are listed below:

Final Scene 121

Mr. Li and Mr. Shen both have great reputations, and it was a rare opportunity to meet this time. More than fifty men and women who admired their names went to watch, and the billiards room was almost impossible to accommodate. They admired the skill of the ball in silence. Before the game, the hall specially photographed for it. The game started at 6:15. In the first ten shots, Mr. Li took the lead, scoring 5, 6, 3, 2, 3, 0, 1, and 7 points, for a total of 140 points. Mr. Shen scored 2, 3, 2, and 0 points, for a total of 61 points. In the next ten shots, Mr. Li scored 231 points, while Mr. Shen only scored 138. By the 25th shot, Mr. Shen had calmed down and used his superb skills, scoring 48 points all the way. At this time, there was a spring of ambition to create, but the cue tip missed its eye, leaving a great opportunity for others to benefit. Mr. Li handled it properly and soon regained what he had lost and surpassed it. The loss of this opportunity was huge for Mr. Shen, and it was impossible to try to save it. The best of Mr. Li that night served as his last three shots. At that time, Mr. Li had 600 points and Mr. Shen had 345 points. With the three shots, Mr. Li finished with 700 points and reached the target score. Mr. Shen only reached 349 points. The applause announced the end of the game. Referee Hu Yunlai, Officer Zhu Zhuangwu.

Two Highest Records

Li's 5, 6, 3, 2, 2, 0, 6, 0, 6, 1, 5, 8. Shen's 2, 3, 2, 0, 2, 6, 2, 1, 4, 8, 3, 6.

With a total of 58 shots, Mr. Li averaged slightly over 11 points per shot, and Mr. Xu averaged slightly over 5 points per shot.
