Standard Flour Prices Decline Consistently 184

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the market for all months consistently showed a weakening and declining trend. The weather has turned clear again, and the season is busy with planting. It is expected that the new wheat harvest can be fully covered in three or four days. In terms of the year's harvest, the north and south regions have a clear shortage and a hidden surplus. At the time of harvest, the weather is good, and the wheat's condition is unusually dry and clean. The source will surely see a surge in supply. Therefore, people's hearts are naturally shifting and loosening step by step. Moreover, the actual sales groups in the north are not optimistic, so the later steps may re-present a soft image. As a result, this month fell two cents compared to the previous period. July fell two and a half cents, August and September fell two cents and seven mils, and October fell two cents and a half. November fell two cents and seven mils.

This Month's Wheat Plummets One Dime 185

Yesterday, the futures wheat market declined across all months during both the morning and afternoon sessions, with this month experiencing the most significant drop. This was primarily due to a slight decrease of approximately two jiao in the reported prices of foreign wheat. Additionally, the favorable weather conditions naturally inclined the general sentiment towards a softening of the market. Although some operators held substantial long positions for this month's settlement, the new wheat harvest is now complete, and based on the quality of the wheat arriving, it is considered to be between average and good. Initially, resistance was maintained, but eventually, even the major long positions started to unwind, leading to a sharp decline in market prices. The drop was particularly steep. July and August also weakened, while September and later months showed greater stability. Consequently, this month plummeted by one dime compared to the previous week, July fell by seven fen, August fell by six fen, September and October fell by four fen, and November fell by three fen. The new wheat market has seen a continuous influx of supplies in recent days, and the quality is considered to be good. Yesterday, over 900 packages of Nanjing Taipingfu wheat were opened, priced between 3.92 taels and 3.90 taels, and were purchased by Shenda.

Youth Forum

Dedicate "Violent Storm" to the Modern Theater Scene 187

— Tian Niu

Some say that relying on aesthetic troupes in various places to shoulder the burden of China's theatrical movement is useless. Public performances by motley crews once or twice a year can never achieve any artistic success. Therefore, to give Chinese theatrical art considerable development, it is necessary for the great educators to awaken and add a theater department to each university or specialized school to cultivate basic Actors or Dramatists. But everything in China is extremely lacking. All education has reached a state of bankruptcy. Who would still pay attention to theater education? In such a large China, the only ones who have made achievements in training theatrical art are Ouyang Yuqian's Drama School in Guangdong, Xiong Fo'er's Department of Drama at the Art Academy in Beiping, and Jiao Juyin's Opera School. In addition, Jiangsu, which can be considered culturally developed, does not yet have this organization. The only thing that can be slightly comforting is the Department of Drama specially set up by the Provincial Educational College to train talents for mass education. Drama is art, and the realm of art cannot be defined by education. Those who advocate aesthetic supremacy, Art For Art's Sake, say so. Therefore, the Department of Drama of the Provincial Educational College, which uses drama as a tool for mass education, naturally cannot satisfy the desires of ordinary artists because it has such a limitation. But to speak in one aspect, apart from formal classroom training, there is also an experimental stage for their testing opportunities. Their progress is naturally much faster than that of the aesthetic troupes. The person in charge of this department is the drama expert, Mr. Gu Jianchen. According to his personal proposition, the masses and the drama should not absolutely accommodate the masses. Therefore, the plays he directs almost based on his above assertion. He is for advocating dramatic art.

He said that art should be popularised and the masses should be artistic, in short, that is not to cater to any aspect. In order to realize his proposition, Mr. Gu has directed many scripts. The most successful are Blood Flower Paying Back a Patriotic Heart and The Unfinished Tombstone. Because they are about to finish this semester, there are exhibitions of achievements. Therefore, there is a public performance. Originally, I wanted to play the fan of the young lady. Later, because there were some problems with the candidates, I re-arranged Mr. Gu's own recent three-act tragedy, Violent Storm. Mr. Gu has always had a weird temper and is unwilling to direct his own plays. His reason is that directing other people's plays must be done with some speculation and effort to gain artistic progress. If you direct your own plays, you will have less of this opportunity. But this time, in order to choose a good script, I had to risk doing it. The script of Violent Storm has not yet been published, so few people outside know about it. I read their mimeographed copy at a friend's house and dared to introduce it here. This is a nationalistic drama. The plot roughly describes the conflict between the Chinese and Japanese nations, with Manchuria and Mongolia as the background, and a Korean woman as the main thread of the whole play. The young man Yang Zhiqin gathers comrades to implement the plan to develop Manchuria and Mongolia, but it is destroyed by the Japanese. The map planning book and other things are lost. Yang Zhiqin was wronged. Not only was he abandoned by the masses, but his fiancee also cancelled his engagement with him. Outside rumors pointed out that he was tempted by the Japanese, so he got the title of traitor. He had nowhere to tell. His heart disease was hurt. Fortunately, Ono Umeko, who thought she was a Japanese woman, knew that her mother was actually Korean, so she admitted to the Chinese and brought back the stolen map and planning book. But the poor young man Yang Zhiqin had already become insane and committed suicide. Later, the Korean girl also died in the hands of the Japanese. The plot of this drama is very tortuous, and there are many shocking pens. It can be described with the old saying that there is no way out of the mountains and rivers, and there is another village. The dialogue at the end has a lot of strength, which can show the cruelty and unreasonableness of Japanese imperialists and the pain of being killed after being used.

Shinjiro (standing at the door, aggressive) Umeko, you have done a good deed.

Camping 188

— Bing She

Umeko (surprised but immediately calm and composed) What good deed did I do?

Shinjiro Where did you take that thing? Find it quickly.

Umeko (candidly) Where we took it from should be returned there.

Shinjiro What are you talking about? You left, and the thing disappeared. I knew it was your trick, so I immediately stuck you here. Where's the thing you took?

Umeko It's right here. It has returned to Chinese hands. You can't take it back anymore.

Shinjiro But you can't not love your country...

Umeko It is precisely because I love my country that I do this. Look at the clothes I am wearing now. Your intelligence will tell you who I am. I am a Korean. I want to love our Korea and no longer love your Japan. You Japanese specialize in using us Koreans to fight against the Chinese. The sacrifice is ours and the benefit is yours. I have been fooled enough times. I can understand myself now.

Shinjiro Nonsense! How dare you say you are not Japanese?

Umeko How can I not be Japanese? Now I can't tell you, but there is one thing I can tell you, simply put, it is the two words (benevolence) and (compassion). Do you Japanese have these two words? For example, this time I was fooled into doing something that I am sorry for the Chinese, which hurt Yang Zhiqin... At that time, my conscience discovered that God's mercy was moving in my blood vessels. At first, someone rumored that I was Korean and I didn't believe it, but now I can suddenly discover that you Japanese don't have the conscience and the mercy of God, which proves that I am indeed Korean and not a Japanese with only cruelty (look at my clothes) You see, I feel so comfortable wearing my own country's clothes.

They - Educational Academy - have a Suzhou girl, Miss Ye Yunzhen, who is short and has a round face. She played the Japanese very successfully in a patriotic heart and an unfinished tombstone. Therefore, Ono Umeko, the Korean girl who is considered Japanese in Violent Storm, will still be played by her. Naturally, she will be competent and happy. This drama is scheduled to be performed at the school on the 13th and 14th of this month. After the performance, I may write another report on the performance.

Book Reviews

Modern Public Finance 190

— Shu Yuan

Author: Zhao Zubian Publisher: Guanghua Bookstore

The financial phenomena of each era are sufficient to influence the financial theories of each era. This book is prefixed with the word "Modern" because it studies modern political principles and principles. This is a scientific book with a sense of the times. China's current finances are very chaotic, so that the national power is declining and the people's livelihood is in trouble. It is all because financial science has not been clarified and promoted. The author is a caring person, so this book is a guide for modern financiers. There is a need to introduce it.

The whole book is divided into five chapters: General Theory, Expenditure Theory, Revenue Theory, Revenue and Expenditure Matching Theory, Financial Administration Theory, and Local Finance Theory.

The general theory describes the characteristics, evolution, current situation and future trends of finance, which are all pre-requisites for financial scholars. This method of outlining the main points first allows readers to have a clear concept of financial science, which is also a feature of this book. The essence of financial science in Section 4 of General Theory 1 is even more the backbone of the whole book. Since financial science is a systematic study of financial principles and principles, its essence certainly cannot go beyond the scope of finance. The content of the scope of finance is expenditure, revenue, the actual matching of revenue and expenditure, and the formal matching and management of revenue and expenditure. Financial science is the study of the principles of expenditure, so there is expenditure theory. It is the study of the principles of revenue, so there is revenue theory. It is the study of the actual matching of revenue and expenditure, so there is revenue and expenditure matching theory or public debt theory. It is the study of the formal matching and management of revenue and expenditure, so there is budget theory, current accounting theory, and final accounting theory, or collectively referred to as financial administration theory. Therefore, the author divides financial science into expenditure theory, revenue theory, revenue and expenditure matching theory, and financial administration theory, plus local finance theory is the most suitable for the scope of modern financial science. As for the order of arrangement, there are also those who hold different opinions, such as first using financial administration theory or simply calling financial administration theory budget theory and then after expenditure theory. There are many theories, each with its own reasons. The author of this book designs the current national finance based on one year as the standard, so it still follows the order of common sense and is named as expenditure theory, revenue theory, revenue and expenditure matching theory, financial administration theory, and local finance theory. The reason for such an arrangement is that finance is based on the principle of measuring expenditure for income. It should first be expenditure theory, then revenue theory. Finance is based on the principle of matching revenue and expenditure, and the matching of revenue and expenditure is actually different from the form. There is no way to attach form to reality, and there is no way to apply reality without form. Reality is revenue and expenditure matching. Form is financial administration. Therefore, it is followed by revenue and expenditure matching theory, and then financial administration theory. Local finance is the result of the development of local autonomy in recent times, and its theory is completely based on the theory of national finance, but there are minor differences. Therefore, putting local finance theory behind this book is exactly as it should be.

The first chapter, Expenditure Theory, Expenditure is the money paid by the country to use labor and objects within a fiscal year in order to fulfill its duties. That is, the country's payment of currency for the price of required economic goods. It studies the facts about this expenditure theory in order to discover its general principles and to provide us with a basis for understanding whether various expenditures are appropriate and to assist in reorganizing finances. The position of expenditure theory in financial science is the same as that of consumption theory in economics. It is the purpose of the whole and the main point of everything. If there is no expenditure theory, other parts such as revenue will become meaningless actions. To study expenditure, we must first know the nature of expenditure. There are two theories about the nature of expenditure: one is the harmful theory of expenditure and the other is the beneficial theory of expenditure. This issue has been studied since the 18th century, and there are many different opinions to this day. The author describes in detail the consumption of the British orthodox school, the production theory of the historical school, and the half-consumption and half-production theory of the modern eclectic school. Therefore, we can better understand the economic nature of expenditure theory. The principles of expenditure are divided into political, financial, economic, and social, which can also be summarized. The classification of expenditure is also extremely complicated. There are usually two classification methods: deductive and inductive. The former method is very simple, and it is usually a dichotomy. The latter method is more complicated, and it is usually a division of more than two points. The former is theoretical and the latter is factual. The author refers to the two theories and divides expenditure into historical, economic, political, and financial, which are simple and appropriate for scholars.

The most important chapter in the expenditure chapter is the research method of expenditure. The methods of researching expenditure are nothing more than deduction and induction. The former is to seek facts with theory and the latter is to seek theory with facts. The former must have a correct concept as the basis and the latter must have correct facts or figures as the basis. However, the results of studying the inductive method are mostly flow statistics. In other words, the results of the inductive method of expenditure research must be expenditure statistics. Each country has its own expenditure statistics. If we want to find out the general trend of expenditure in various countries, we must collect and compare various statistics. However, the content and value of the statistics of various countries often vary greatly and are difficult to compare. The author specifically points out the reasons for not being easy to compare.

1. The classification of expenses and the scope of each category in the budget preparation of various countries are often different, so it is difficult to compare.

2. Although the principle of budget unification is a publicly recognized principle in finance, in practice, special budgets are often established outside the general budget, so the truth of expenditure cannot be explored.

3. The existence or absence of supplementary budgets and the amount of them are also sufficient to make it difficult to know the truth of general expenditure, at least to make the investigation difficult.

4. The implementation period of the budget should be when the national treasury has more income and less expenditure, but in practice, the starting period of the fiscal year in various countries is different, resulting in many differences in the impact of expenditure on the economy in various countries, so it is also difficult to compare.

5. The content of financial expenses in the expenditure statistics of various countries is often different, and the amount is often different, so the superficial calculation of the expenditure statistics of various countries is not enough to represent the actual truth of the national expenditure.

6. Modern local autonomy is developed and local expenses are also very important, but local expenditure statistics are not very complete, so it can be seen that it is not correct to compare only with national expenditure.

7. The expenditure statistics of various countries in the United Nations are also incomplete, so it is difficult to study the truth of the entire expenditure by only discussing the expenditure of the United Nations.

8. In countries with unclear politics, the surface figures in the budget are often untrue.

With the above difficulties and actual conditions, we can naturally pay special attention when using this kind of statistics.

The second chapter, Revenue Theory, The total amount of currency received by the central government or local groups for the treasury within a fiscal year to meet expenditures is called revenue. The author observes the evolution of revenue from a historical perspective and divides it into four periods: (1) the period of official income, (2) the period of privilege income, (3) the period of tax income, and (4) the period of official industry income. The classification of revenue is very complicated by various schools, and there is no need to attach importance to it in theory. The author advocates the dichotomy of revenue. This classification has about six types, namely (1) automatic income and passive income, (2) public law income and private law income, (3) micro-tax income and industrial income, (4) ordinary income, accidental income, and extraordinary income, (5) current income and temporary income, (6) public economic income and private economic income. Among the above six classifications, the author also advocates using the sixth type to study revenue because revenue is composed of current income and temporary income, and the sixth type is exactly what explains current income. According to the above theory, the author classifies revenue as follows:

(A) Current revenue (a) Income of public economy (A) Political affairs income 1. Handling fee 2. Usage fee 3. Special donation 4. Illegal money (B) Tax (b) Income of private economy (A) Official property income (B) Official industry income (B) Temporary revenue (a) Purely temporary income (A) Private donation (B) War compensation (C) Confiscation of unclaimed property (b) Predetermined temporary income (A) Increase tax (B) Raise public debt (C) Sales of official land

With such a classification, we can understand it at a glance without looking at the explanation.

This book describes the theory, principles, and classification of taxes in detail in the discussion of public economic income in this chapter, and discusses the income tax, property tax, income tax, circulation tax, and consumption tax separately in the discussion of various taxes, which is particularly concise.

The third chapter, Revenue and Expenditure Matching Theory, The principle of national finance is to match revenue and expenditure. In other words, current revenue must be used to fill current expenditure, and temporary revenue must only be used to fill temporary expenditure. Within a considerable range, there are also those who use current revenue to fill temporary expenditure. In short, in budget making, we must never make revenue and expenditure offset each other and still have a surplus or shortage. However, in reality, if there is a surplus, there is no problem. The most relevant thing is the financial shortage. The method to solve this shortage problem is public debt, so some people also call the theory of revenue and expenditure matching the theory of public debt. In other words, there is nothing else to discuss in the theory of revenue and expenditure matching besides the discussion of public debt. This book succinctly describes the meaning, essence, methods, types and consolidation of public debt. The most important thing is that it explains the advantages and disadvantages of issuing public debt very clearly. Financiers can refer to it to know where to go.

The fifth chapter, Local Finance Theory, Local finance is the study of the finance of local groups, divided into local expenditure theory, local revenue theory, revenue and expenditure matching theory, and financial administration theory. The special points of local expenditure theory are listed as follows: (1) Local expenditure should try to reduce administrative expenses and expand business expenses. (2) Local expenditure should be restricted by central laws and regulations. (3) Local expenditure should pay special attention to the implementation of social policies. (4) Local expenditure should be based on current expenditure as the principle, and temporary expenditure can only be carried out when it is absolutely necessary. (5) Local expenditure should regard expenditures outside the budget as unexpected abuses. (6) Local expenditure sometimes has the expenditure of sharing money and assisting money. The former is the cost of the central government that is shared by various local groups, and the latter is the mutual assistance of local groups.

In addition, local revenue and expenditure matching are largely the same as those of the country, but the special differences between local financial administration and national financial administration are also things that local finance researchers must know. The records are as follows: (1) Local budgets are always under the supervision of the state, and the state has the power to revise and enforce them. (2) Although the local autonomy laws all have provisions on the accounting system, they are only general and not sufficient for application, so the interpretation of analogy must be used in local financial administration. The national accounting law and auditing law can be applied to what is not provided for in the local autonomy laws. (3) The fiscal year should be the same as the national year, but the starting period of the local year should be appropriate one or two months after the national budget is determined. (4) Local income and expenditure are very simple, and the period for sorting out receipts and payments should be shorter. (5) In addition to the general budget, local finances often have many special budgets because local income is mainly derived from industry. (6) The scope of local finance is very small and predictable. We should try our best to avoid proposing supplementary budgets.

Finally, let me say that this book is a guide for modern financiers.

Shanghai Market

Business News 191

Well-known calligraphers and painters Wang Zhongshan, Zhang Yuguang, Ye Weishen, Gao Shangzhi, Xu Xiaochun, Wang Fengxian, Shen Yizhai, Guo Jilan, and others, in response to the needs of society as the summer season arrives, have each created convenient scrolls. Together, they will exhibit numerous landscape paintings, bird-and-flower paintings, and animal paintings from June 9th to 11th at the Ningbo Native Place Association. Additionally, various painting manuals from each artist will be displayed and sold.

The Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau, located at the corner of Shilu Road on Sanma Road, is a revolutionary new store that has risen to prominence. In addition to gaining the trust of society with its two special features of selecting excellent goods and setting low prices, it also excels in training all its employees to treat customers with the five virtues of humility, kindness, gentleness, courtesy, and concession as the sole method. Therefore, the bureau's recent excellent business performance has set a new record unmatched by major silk and satin stores. It is reported that the large batch of seasonal summer goods that the bureau recently received has already been sold out. Now, they have added new products such as woven flower georgette, woven flower voile, woven flower gold silk, woven flower silver silk, specially made floral Western Indian georgette, Palas, plain crepe, and other items, displayed in the windows with a dazzling array. Customers are welcome to select and purchase.

The Jinxing Tie Company, located at No. 422, Baoshan Road, Baotong Road Intersection, Zhabei, declares that its products have always been known for their excellence. Recently, to facilitate the academic circles in the Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Zhenru areas, they have added a

Branch store specializing in the sale of ties, shirts, suits, separate sports shirts, trousers, etc. produced by the company. A big sale starts today for fourteen days. 1931-style summer ties are only priced at fifty cents each. This is truly a good opportunity for all circles to purchase clothing and separate items. The company held a major sale once last year, which was very short-lived, and many people regretted missing it.

The Guanshengyuan Food Company on Nanjing Road declares that the company's recent seasonal food product, zongzi (sticky rice dumplings), is the most popular. Based on the experience of making Cantonese-style zongzi that suit Shanghai people's taste over the years, a large quantity of products has now been produced. Flavors include lotus seed paste, egg yolk, ham, salted meat, and fresh meat. Prices range from one dime to several dimes each and are packaged in art boxes at no extra charge. Sales have been very brisk at the company's main store in Japan, as well as the old store in Jiumudi, the branch store on Henan Road, and the branch store on Fada Road.
